\boldsymbol{v}) - (\boldsymbol{e_{\mu}} \cdot \boldsymbol{v})}. \\ &amp;= \sum_{\mu} \frac{[R(\boldsymbol{e_{\mu}}, \boldsymbol{v}) \boldsymbol{v}] \cdot \boldsymbol{e_{\mu}}}{(1) (1) - (0)} \\ &amp;= \sum_{\mu} v^{\nu} v^{\sigma} [R(\boldsymbol{e_{\mu}}, \boldsymbol{e_{\nu}}) \boldsymbol{e_{\sigma}}] \cdot \boldsymbol{e_{\mu}} \\ &amp;= v^{\nu} v^{\sigma} \sum_{\mu} R^{\lambda}{}_{\sigma \mu \nu} \boldsymbol{e_{\lambda}} \cdot \boldsymbol{e_{\mu}} \\ &amp;= v^{\nu} v^{\sigma} \sum_{\mu} R^{\lambda}{}_{\sigma \mu \nu} g_{\lambda \mu} \\ &amp;= v^{\nu} v^{\sigma} R^{\mu}{}_{\sigma \mu \nu} \\
